>                                   )}

>                                       1,

>                                     );

>                                     updateTradeCartQty(row.listingId, next);
>                                   }}
>                                 />

>                                 <button className="ghost" onClick={() => removeTradeCartItem(row.listingId)}>
>                                   Sepetten cikar
>                                 </button>
>                                 <button className="ghost" onClick={() => quickOfferForListing(row.listing)}>
>                                   Hemen teklif
>                                 </button>
>                               </div>
>                             </li>
>                           ))}
>                         </ul>
